When live remote reads are unavailable inside the local Node sandbox, it falls back to local `refs/remotes/origin/main` with a warning. This keeps the tracked external proof commit historical while preventing a stale local HEAD from being reported as release-ready. |

## 2026-07-03 Mobile Android Store Permission Minimization

| Area                                  | Path                                                                                                                                | Status        | Verification                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Notes                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| ------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Android store permission minimization | `apps/mobile/app.config.ts`, `apps/mobile/src/config/__tests__/mobile-e2e-contract.test.ts`, `docs/codex/08_FILE_COMPLETION_LOG.md` | Verified PASS | RED `corepack pnpm --filter @salary-hijacking/mobile run test -- src/config/__tests__/mobile-e2e-contract.test.ts --runInBand`: FAIL because broad storage/overlay permissions were not blocked; GREEN same command: PASS, 1 suite and 5 tests. Broader verification is recorded in the final task report. | Added Expo `blockedPermissions` for `READ_EXTERNAL_STORAGE`, `WRITE_EXTERNAL_STORAGE`, and `SYSTEM_ALERT_WINDOW` so regenerated native Android manifests remove broad storage/overlay access. This keeps the finance app permission surface focused on server-authoritative finance, notifications, biometric access, vibration, internet, and deep links. Production AAB, native E2E, Play Console proof, and runtime Cloudflare/secret evidence remain release gates. |

## Update Rule

When completing a work slice, append or update a row with:

- path,
- status,
- exact command,
- PASS/FAIL,
- remaining blockers.
